[{"id":29488,"date":"2023-04-05T15:29:18","date_gmt":"2023-04-05T07:29:18","guid":{"rendered":"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/?p=29488"},"modified":"2023-08-01T09:46:20","modified_gmt":"2023-08-01T01:46:20","slug":"just-to-be-on-the-safe-side","status":"publish","type":"post","link":"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/just-to-be-on-the-safe-side\/","title":{"rendered":"Just to be on the Safe Side"},"content":{"rendered":"
    \n
  • \n
    The importance of safeguarding the wellbeing, health and safety of people has always been an imperative for us at Sunway.<\/h5>\n<\/li>\n
  • \n
    Across our multiple business divisions, Sunway prioritises a safe working environment physically, mentally and emotionally \u2013 so that our people can work more efficiently and productively.<\/h5>\n<\/li>\n<\/ul>\n

    Aside from fair remuneration and work-life balance, workplace safety<\/strong><\/a> is highly sought after by jobseekers today. A healthy workplace environment will bring a more positive atmosphere to employees, thus encouraging them to yield better results for the organisation as a whole.<\/p>\n

    As a people-first organisation, Sunway \u2013 boasting a 16,000-strong workforce worldwide \u2013 has vast experience in implementing effective policies and strategies that is valued by both employer and employee.<\/p>\n

    This has evidently borne fruit, leading to several recognitions at the 2022 Malaysian Society for Occupational Health and Safety Awards (MSOSH) for Sunway Malls, Sunway Medical Centre and Sunway Construction (SunCon) \u2013 with SunCon and Sunway Pyramid leading the way with a Gold Class I award respectively.<\/p>\n

    Sunway raked in several wins at the MSOSH Awards 2022.<\/p><\/div>\n

    Enforcing the best practices for Occupational Health, Safety and Environment (OHSE) cannot be achieved by leaders alone. This is why Sunway has established a Group OHSE Council<\/a><\/strong> to discuss, improve and implement OHSE matters to protect employees. Chaired by Sunway Group president Tan Sri Chew Chee Kin, the council meets once every three months to discuss matters raised by each business division and serve as an avenue for employees to have their voices heard<\/strong><\/a>.<\/p>\n

    In conjunction with World Day for Safety and Health at Work celebrated annually on 28 April, we speak to our leaders in these award-winning divisions on what safety means to them \u2013 and how this makes Sunway the workplace of choice year after year.<\/p>\n

    Preserving a culture of safety <\/strong><\/h3>\n

    \u201cDatang selamat, kerja selamat dan pulang selamat.\u201d <\/em><\/p><\/blockquote>\n

    That is the motto that Sunway Construction (SunCon) lives by, and Kalaiselvan Selvaraja, SunCon\u2019s Environment, Safety and Health (ESH) general manager elaborates that the safety of each employee is prioritised through proper planning, effective risk management and precautionary measures to protect them and their respective stakeholders.<\/p>\n

    \u201cThe construction industry is most commonly referred to as a \u201chigh-risk sector\u201d of the economy, primarily because our workers are exposed to a wide range of hazards daily. Health and safety at work to me is achievable at its highest standard when we are able to adopt and inculcate safety as a culture and self-regulatory practices are in place within an organisation and in every individual,\u201d he shares.<\/p><\/blockquote>\n

    Kalaiselvan shares that proper planning, effective risk management and precautionary measures must be put in place.<\/p><\/div>\n

    Captain Mohd Shahrizal, Sunway Medical Centre (SMC)\u2019s ESH manager perceives safety as the responsibility of not just one individual, but all layers of the organisation.<\/p>\n

    \u201cGood health and safety management comes from strong leadership that systematically manages safety and health operations based on guidelines set by relevant local authorities involving managers, employees, suppliers, contractors and customers. The result of this efficient management allows employees, tenants, suppliers, visitors and patients to always feel safe within our businesses.\u201d<\/p><\/blockquote>\n

    SMC strives to ensure that the safety and comfort level of all employees and patients was upheld during the pandemic.<\/p><\/div>\n

    Jason Chin, Sunway Malls\u2019 general manager for operations echoes this sentiment, and believes that employee empowerment should be taken into account.<\/p>\n

    \u201cEmployee participation is extremely essential in order to create an environment with the least health and safety risks. It is key to ensure the company builds a caring, humane and safe environment not just for stakeholders, but for ourselves. At Sunway Malls, we take health and safety practices seriously to boost the morale and the productivity of our employees.\u201d<\/p><\/blockquote>\n

    As a healthcare institution that serves the nation greatly, SMC is aware of the importance of mental health amongst its employees. With stricter SOPs in line and the guidelines set out by the Ministry of Health (MOH), SMC began introducing employee health awareness programmes as well as continuous training throughout the period.<\/p>\n

    \u201cStaff health assessment is also carried out from time to time to monitor and ensure that it is at the best level. All planned programmes and implementation activities are taken as a step to provide the best service to customers,\u201d Captain Mohd Shahrizal shares.<\/p><\/blockquote>\n

    Rewinding back to the height of the pandemic, Sunway Malls made headlines for providing its retail partners a 14-day rent waiver, followed by further rental assistance totalling RM150 million and a RM5 million marketing campaign to drive sales. However, there was still much to be done as the malls were under much scrutiny by the authorities, public and netizens. Hygiene and safety were a top priority, and this applied to the employees as well.<\/p>\n

    Shopper and employee confidence was a main focal point for Sunway Malls.<\/p><\/div>\n

    \u201cOn top of introducing campaigns such as \u201cYour Safe Space, Our Safe Space\u201d and \u201cKita<\/em> Support Kita<\/em>\u201d to build consumer confidence, we also collaborated with our business partners to reward frontline workers, thanking them for their unwavering dedication during the difficult period. Together with Group-level management, we encouraged vaccination amongst all employees and tenants, expanding the understanding of herd immunity to prevent the virus from spreading,\u201d he shares.<\/p><\/blockquote>\n

    When the world came to a standstill, the construction industry was one of the hardest hit as curbing the spread of the virus amongst workers in a labour-intensive industry was a major challenge.<\/p>\n

    \u201cTo power through, SunCon established a Business Continuity Plan (BCP) to manage our workplaces, ensuring our workforce is protected at all times and risk of infection is minimised as business resumed post-Movement Control Order (MCO). When we discovered that workers’ quarters posed a high risk of COVID-19 spread, the enforcement of Act 446 was timely to prevent an outbreak within our premises. The pandemic accelerated an opportunity for us to move forward with digitalised initiatives to help minimise disruptions of our work processes,\u201d Kalaiselvan notes.<\/p><\/blockquote>\n

    Highlighting the S in ESG <\/strong><\/h3>\n

    Kalaiselvan adds that setting a high bar for these OHSE standards<\/strong><\/a> has allowed them to adopt a culture of responsibility, accountability, taking ownership and working with integrity.<\/p>\n

    \u201cA healthier workforce is a more productive workforce, and safeguarding this wellbeing is an important aspect of the social pillar in ESG.\u201d<\/p><\/blockquote>\n

    At SMC, regular ESG-related training is carried out for staff to ensure that they understand and are responsible for Sunway\u2019s commitment to advancing the UN-SDGs.<\/p>\n

    Captain Shahrizal shares that regular training is carried out for employees to understand the Group\u2019s ESG and sustainability commitments.<\/p><\/div>\n

    Jason concludes by reiterating Sunway\u2019s emphasis on establishing holistic policies and placing people at its core.<\/p>\n

    Jason notes that Sunway walks the talk by adhering to best practices and standards that are reinforced by health and safety audits and reports.<\/p><\/div>\n

    \u201cBy creating a safe, healthy and inclusive environment for our people, Sunway reduces risk exposures which in turn promotes SDG 8: Decent Work and Economic Growth of the UN-SDGs and the social aspect of ESG. Any company can set policies and requirements, but Sunway goes beyond by ensuring that continuous audits are reported according to standards and regulations and becomes part of everyone\u2019s daily tasks.\u201d<\/p><\/blockquote>\n","protected":false},"excerpt":{"rendered":"

the Digital Gender Divide"},"content":{"rendered":"<p>Whether you are pursuing an online course, using social media to promote a business, or paying for purchases with your e-wallet, the use of digital technology has revolutionised the way we live and work today.<\/p>\n<p>Unfortunately, the reality is that not everyone has the opportunity to experience the transformational potential of digital technology.<\/p>\n<p>The United Nations\u2019 International Telecommunication Union (ITU) estimates that 2.9 billion people worldwide have never used the Internet, the majority of which are women. This limits opportunities for women to learn online and improve their livelihoods.<\/p>\n<p>Women are also underrepresented in the information and communications technology (ICT) industry, holding 15% of the STEM (science, technology, engineering and mathematics) jobs; men were four times more likely to be ICT specialists.<\/p>\n<p>Recognising this, the United Nations has commemorated the recent International Women\u2019s Day 2023 with the theme, \u2018DigitALL: Innovation and technology for gender equality\u2019, to address the need for inclusive as well as <a href=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/join-the-robo-lution\/\"><strong>transformative technology<\/strong><\/a> and digital education.<\/p>\n<h3><strong>The future of everyone is at stake<\/strong><\/h3>\n<p>Considering that women comprise almost 50 percent of the global population, achieving gender equality and empowering all females is not just an aspiration, but a prerequisite to attain the United Nations Sustainable Development Goals (UN-SDGs).<\/p>\n<p>As agents of change in their families, communities and countries, increasing the voice and participation of women in positions of leadership, labour force and education, will not only benefit women, but everyone \u2013 unlocking the door to a brighter future.<\/p>\n<p>Women typically invest a higher proportion of their earnings in their families and communities than men. Their economic participation also accelerates development, helps overcome poverty, and improves children\u2019s access to education, healthcare and nutrition, said the Organisation for Economic Co-operation and Development (OECD).<\/p>\n<p>In the digital era, creating a level playing field for women means equipping them with the digital tools, access and knowledge they need to fully participate in and benefit from the digital economy.<\/p>\n<p>Greater inclusion of women as users and leaders of digital financial services (fintech) also fosters better performance of fintech firms, which is critical to economic growth.<\/p>\n<div id=\"attachment_29439\" style=\"width: 1210px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-29439\" class=\"wp-image-29439 size-full\" src=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/03\/KLB_2969-1.jpg\" alt=\"Sunway staff of three females and one male having an online meeting regarding FinTech and analysing data, with graphs and papers at their desk\" width=\"1200\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/03\/KLB_2969-1-200x133.jpg 200w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/03\/KLB_2969-1-600x400.jpg 600w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/03\/KLB_2969-1-768x512.jpg 768w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/03\/KLB_2969-1-800x533.jpg 800w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/03\/KLB_2969-1-942x628.jpg 942w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/03\/KLB_2969-1.jpg 1200w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" \/><p id=\"caption-attachment-29439\" class=\"wp-caption-text\">The inclusivity of all genders will only lead to a victory for all.<\/p><\/div>\n<p>McKinsey Global Institute research estimated that if women were given an identical role in labour markets as men, they could contribute to as much as US$28 trillion (RM127.7 trillion), or a 26% growth, to the global annual gross domestic product (GDP) in 2025.<\/p>\n<blockquote><p>\u201cWomen\u2019s financial inclusion is one of the many powerful levers that can boost gender equality and, at the same time, raise economic growth, financial stability, and income equality. But we can\u2019t make progress if we don\u2019t truly understand the realities of women\u2019s lives,\u201d the IMF noted.<\/p>\n<p>\u201cWith more inclusivity, we will become a society that is more empathetic towards each other\u2019s needs and more innovative in coming up with solutions to elevate the community. This will lead to an increase in productivity and income equality,\u201d said Melissa Hashim, senior manager of creative marketing at Sunway Malls.<\/p><\/blockquote>\n<div id=\"attachment_29425\" style=\"width: 1210px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-29425\" class=\"size-full wp-image-29425\" id=\"caption-attachment-29425\" class=\"wp-caption-text\">Melissa Hashim, senior manager of creative marketing at Sunway Malls.<\/p><\/div>\n<h3><strong>Creating a more equitable world<\/strong><\/h3>\n<p>Activists argue that there cannot be gender equality without gender equity \u2013 acknowledging that every individual has different starting points and being fair in meeting their specific needs.<\/p>\n<p><strong><a href=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/workplace-inclusiveness-and-diversity-a-people-first-approach\/\">Recognising and celebrating our differences<\/a> <\/strong>\u2013 seeing them as strengths to leverage instead of threats \u2013 as well as providing more conducive environments to support the needs of colleagues from different circumstances, are some ways of achieving gender equality, said Teh Ji-Lian, head of talent management & employer branding of Group human resources at Sunway Group.<\/p>\n<div id=\"attachment_29421\" style=\"width: 1210px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-29421\" class=\"size-full wp-image-29421\" class=\"wp-caption-text\">Teh Ji-Lian, head of talent management & employer branding of Group human resources at Sunway Group.<\/p><\/div>\n<blockquote><p>\u201cAt Sunway, we truly believe in meritocracy and providing equal opportunities to learn and grow. There is more to be done to help our leaders be more aware of unconscious bias, bring it to consciousness and having a broader dialogue about it,\u201d said Teh.<\/p><\/blockquote>\n<p>Sunway\u2019s Diversity & Inclusion Policy ensures equal opportunities for all employees irrespective of gender, race or background.<\/p>\n<p>Other Sunway initiatives that reduce the gender gap in the workplace include flexi-hour work policies that allow women to balance work and caregiving responsibilities, as well as nursing rooms at every business division for breastfeeding mothers.<\/p>\n<p>To address the digital gender gap, Sunway is consciously hiring more women with STEM backgrounds, as well as organising digital upskilling initiatives such as 42KL\u2019s Code4Work coding bootcamp in 2022 to increase digital literacy and empower Sunway staff to utilise digital skills to add value to their work.<\/p>\n<p>The <a href=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/to-code-or-not-to-code-42kls-piscine-survivors-sheds-light-on-their-dive\/\"><strong>42KL coding school<\/strong><\/a> at Sunway City Kuala Lumpur plays a key role in advancing digital gender equality by offering tuition-free digital education to students irrespective of their age, gender, religion, culture, geography, economic and educational backgrounds.<\/p>\n<p>Citing 42KL as her biggest inspiration, Sunway Property manager of brand strategy and communications Betty Jane Jelia said that having an avenue to pursue her interest in coding has motivated her to digitally upskill herself.<\/p>\n<div id=\"attachment_29426\" style=\"width: 1210px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-29426\" class=\"size-full wp-image-29426\" src=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/03\/BETTY-JANE.jpeg\" alt=\"Sunway Property As a society, we need to provide women with the opportunity to access them. Only when we all have equal access can we truly reach our fullest potential,\u201d said Betty.<\/p><\/blockquote>\n<p>Ultimately, the fight for gender equality should involve everyone \u2013 private sector, governments as well as individuals \u2013 because the impact of gender inequality affects us all, said Chanratanak Rong, assistant director of group marcomms at Sunway Healthcare Group.<\/p>\n<div id=\"attachment_29427\" style=\"width: 1210px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-29427\" class=\"size-full not an individual sprint, but a team relay race.<\/p>\n<p>With Sunway\u2019s concerted efforts to bridge the digital gender divide, we strive to work together towards the finish line \u2013 fostering Sunway Pyramid Hotel\u2019s long-tenured front office manager.<\/h5>\n<\/li>\n<li>\n<h5>From a part-time waitress trying to make ends meet, to providing a comfortable life for her family, Shanta shares her appreciation of Sunway transforming her life \u2013 both personally and professionally \u2013 and how Sunway has and is still empowering her growth throughout her 20-year journey with the Group.<\/h5>\n<\/li>\n<\/ul>\n<p>Everyone loves an inspirational \u2013 of a person who has risen above the tide, against all odds, and to finally emerge on the other side better, stronger and happier than ever.<\/p>\n<p>This is the story of Shanta Vijiasundram, currently a front office manager at Sunway Pyramid Hotel.<\/p>\n<\/div><div class=\"fusion-text fusion-text-2\"><div first impression of Sunway Pyramid Hotel rests on the shoulders of Shanta.<\/div><\/div><\/li>\n <\/ul>\n <\/div>\n \n <\/div>\n<\/div>\n<\/div><div class=\"fusion-text fusion-text-3\"><p>For 20 years, Shanta has dedicated her time and effort to Sunway.\u00a0 Her journey started while she was still in high school \u2013 where she to take up a part-time job to make ends meet for her family after a tragic loss.<\/p>\n<h3><strong>How it All Began<\/strong><\/h3>\n<blockquote>\n<p><em>\u201cI lost my father when I was 14-years old. Though my mother had just started working in a factory as an operator, it was not enough to support a family of four. I wanted to help \u2013 hence I took a part-time waitressing job to support the financial burdens of my mother,\u201d as Shanta starts her story.<\/em><\/p>\n<\/blockquote>\n<div id=\"attachment_29218\" style=\"width: 1210px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-29218\" class=\"size-full wp-image-29218\" 1200w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" \/><p id=\"caption-attachment-29218\" class=\"wp-caption-text\">Shanta\u2019s first job was at the Avanti Ristorante, an indirect start of Shanta\u2019s Sunway journey.<\/p><\/div>\n<p>Even after completing high school, Shanta worked every afternoon at Avanti Ristorante (<em>famed for its Italian cuisine in the 90s) <\/em>at Sunway Resort Hotel & Spa (now known as <strong><a href=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/malaysias-dream-vacation-reimagined\/\">Sunway Resort Hotel<\/a><\/strong>).<\/p>\n<p>Shanta\u2019s hard work helped cover the educational expenditures of her younger siblings, as well as her own, which was an extreme boost for her family.<\/p>\n<p>Post-SPM however, she dabbled in different industries. But yet, Shanta could not shake off the feeling that the hospitality industry was her true calling.<\/p>\n<blockquote>\n<p><em>\u201cAfter my SPM examination, I had chosen a different career path. However, after a year, I felt a passion towards the hospitality and hotel industry, hence I returned to Sunway Resort Hotel & Spa, continuing to work as a waitress at Avanti,\u201d<\/em><\/p>\n<\/blockquote>\n<p>From a part-time waitress, she worked her way up to becoming a full-time staff at the restaurant. She eventually made the switch to Sunway Hospitality, which kicked off a journey that would change her life in ways that she could never imagine.<\/p>\n<div id=\"attachment_29213\" style=\"width: 1210px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-29213\" class=\"size-full wp-image-29213\" src=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/0G9A2392.jpg\" alt=\"Shanta Vijiasundram, Sunway Pyramid Hotel\u2019s long-tenured front office manager posing in front of the front lit wall at Sunway Pyramid Hotel.\" width=\"1200\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/0G9A2392-200x133.jpg 200w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/0G9A2392-314x209.jpg 314w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/0G9A2392-400x267.jpg 400w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/0G9A2392-600x400.jpg 600w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/0G9A2392-768x512.jpg 768w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/0G9A2392-800x533.jpg 800w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/0G9A2392-942x628.jpg 942w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/0G9A2392.jpg 1200w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" \/><p id=\"caption-attachment-29213\" class=\"wp-caption-text\">Say \u201chi!\u201d to Shanta when you check in!<\/p><\/div>\n<h3><strong>The Highs<\/strong><\/h3>\n<p>Recognising her dedication and drive, Sunway saw an opportunity to help Shanta and further her education, giving her a hand up \u2013 both in her career and in life.<\/p>\n<blockquote>\n<p><em>\u201cMy financial background did not allow me to complete my studies as at a young age, I had to fend for my family. However, Sunway saw the potential in me and sent me for a Diploma in Hotel Management. This was immense as it allowed me to advance my career in the hospitality industry,\u201d said Shanta.<\/em><\/p>\n<\/blockquote>\n<div id=\"attachment_29223\" style=\"width: 1210px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-29223\" class=\"size-full wp-image-29223\" id=\"caption-attachment-29223\" class=\"wp-caption-text\">Giving a hand-up, and never a hand-out.<\/p><\/div>\n<p>Through her passion, determination, drive and now, credentials, Shanta has taken this golden opportunity firmly with both hands. This led to her steady climb up the ranks, attaining the front office manager position at Sunway Pyramid Hotel.<\/p>\n<p><img decoding=\"async\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-29238\" src=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/0G9A2335b.jpg\" alt=\"Shanta at work. Tan, senior managing director of Sunway Group; and of course, to our founder and chairman, Tan Sri Sir Jeffrey Cheah; and to all the leaders who were here at Sunway and gave me the opportunity to enhance my career with the Group,\u201d shared Shanta.<\/em><\/p>\n<\/blockquote>\n<h3><strong>The Lows<\/strong><\/h3>\n<div id=\"attachment_29216\" style=\"width: 1210px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-29216\" class=\"size-full wp-image-29216\" src=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/MicrosoftTeams-image-22.jpg\" alt=\"Empty airport chairs and a glossy floor, with the morning sun beaming down on the chairs.\" width=\"1200\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/MicrosoftTeams-image-22-200x133.jpg 200w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/MicrosoftTeams-image-22-314x209.jpg 314w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/MicrosoftTeams-image-22-400x267.jpg 400w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/MicrosoftTeams-image-22-600x400.jpg 600w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/MicrosoftTeams-image-22-768x512.jpg 768w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/MicrosoftTeams-image-22-800x533.jpg 800w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/MicrosoftTeams-image-22-942x628.jpg 942w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/MicrosoftTeams-image-22.jpg 1200w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" \/><p id=\"caption-attachment-29216\" class=\"wp-caption-text\">The hospitality and tourism industry were among the worst-hit industries during the COVID-19 pandemic.<\/p><\/div>\n<p>The hospitality landscape was one of the worst-hit industries during the pandemic. Border restrictions, a near total lockdown on the <strong><a href=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/how-industries-are-roaring-back-to-spur-tourism\/\">tourism sector<\/a>,<\/strong> the ever-constant fear of the virus lurking about \u2013 it was a tough time.<\/p>\n<div id=\"attachment_29215\" style=\"width: 1210px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-29215\" class=\"size-full wp-image-29215\" src=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/20220805_150502.jpg\" alt=\"Front office staff working to check customers in during COVID-19 period.\" width=\"1200\" height=\"900\" srcset=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/20220805_150502-200x150.jpg https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/20220805_150502-837x628.jpg 837w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/20220805_150502.jpg 1200w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" \/><p id=\"caption-attachment-29215\" class=\"wp-caption-text\">Despite the high risks of COVID-19, Sunway has taken vital steps to ensure the safety of all guests and staff.<\/p><\/div>\n<blockquote>\n<p><em>\u201cWorking during the pandemic and serving guests were real challenges that we experienced together as hospitality staff \u2013 having to work around the new SOPs set by the government, and not to mention catching the virus a looming fear in our minds. But, by working and being there for one another, we managed to get through it and to serve our guests the best we can,\u201d said Shanta.<\/em><\/p>\n<\/blockquote>\n<p>Balancing the financial situation of our hotels during such an unprecedented time was also more crucial than ever. As with any hotel business, the pandemic had adversely impacted room occupancy levels and caused as sharp drop in revenue.\u00a0 It was worrying for hotel employees when news of layoffs and pay cuts were heard across the industry, and even more so when news surfaced that hotels were being permanently closed.<\/p>\n<p>But not in Sunway. It is in our DNA to take care of our people and to ensure their livelihoods are not compromised, owing to our sustainability strategy and adaptability that allows us to weather the pandemic storm well. This allowed us to fulfil our commitment to paying dividends to its shareholders, and most importantly, to ensure that the bread and butter of our staff were unaffected during the pandemic.<\/p>\n<blockquote>\n<p><em>\u201cEvery day, I prayed that there will be no layoffs or salary cuts because each of us has commitments and family. Hence, I thank Sunway because there were no salary cuts nor furloughs during the pandemic, which had allowed us to continue to work with peace of mind,\u201d said a relieved Shanta.<\/em><\/p>\n<\/blockquote>\n<h3><strong>Looking Back<\/strong><\/h3>\n<p>Having achieved 20 excellent years at Sunway, Shanta has experienced a <strong><a href=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/our-brand-evolution-since-1974\/\">wide range of transformations<\/a><\/strong> as part of the Sunway family \u2013 from starting off at Sunway\u2019s sole flagship hotel, Sunway Resort Hotel to the inception of Sunway Pyramid Hotel and Sunway Lagoon Hotel, Shanta has seen how Sunway and its hospitality arm has grown from strength to strength over the decades, leading up to our 50th <a href=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/celebrating-the-golden-anniversary-by-transforming-lives\/\"><strong>anniversary in 2024<\/strong><\/a>.<\/p>\n<p>As such, there is bound to be a memory or two to look back on \u2013 whether bittersweet or fondly.<\/p>\n<blockquote>\n<p>\u201cI appreciate Sunway as it has always been fair in giving opportunities to those who need it, and to not allow race or gender be an obstacle for our careers. Sunway truly walks the talk in its three core values of integrity, humility and excellence,\u201d said Shanta.<\/p>\n<\/blockquote>\n<div id=\"attachment_29222\" style=\"width: 1210px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-29222\" class=\"size-full wp-image-29222\" Sunway at Sunway Resort Hotel.\" width=\"1200\" height=\"1600\" srcset=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2023\/02\/WhatsApp-Image-2022-11-30-at-6.59.17-PM-157x209.jpeg id=\"caption-attachment-29222\" class=\"wp-caption-text\">Celebrating 20 years at Sunway!<\/p><\/div>\n<p>Lifting the curtain behind memory lane, Shanta shares some of her finest moments at Sunway.<\/p>\n<blockquote>\n<p>\u201cMy fondest moment at Sunway was the day I was promoted to manager. I felt like I had accomplished my dream which I held on to since my first day working here,\u201d said Shanta proudly.<\/p>\n<\/blockquote>\n<p>Shanta says that \u2013 and with no hyperbole whatsoever \u2013 everything in her life has changed for the better over the last 20 years, dating back to her time serving customers at Avanti. From being a provider during her teenage years, to achieving her tertiary education and climbing up the ranks and now, being able to provide a comfortable and joyful life for her own family.<\/p>\n<div id=\"attachment_29221\" style=\"width: 1210px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-29221\" class=\"size-full the Scenes of A Spooky Business"},"content":{"rendered":"<ul>\n<li>\n<h5>From being a visitor at the first Nights of Fright to managing the entire event several years later in 2022, Aishah is passionate about delivering excitement and fun to theme park visitors \u2013 even if it means getting a scream or two out of them.<\/h5>\n<\/li>\n<li>\n<h5>As manager of events and entertainment for Sunway Theme Parks (inclusive of Sunway Lagoon and Lost World of Tambun), her day is filled with various tasks to create the best day ever for all guests.<\/h5>\n<\/li>\n<\/ul>\n<p>After a few years of <a href=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/feeling-a-little-uneasy-to-travel-post-covid\/\"><strong>restrictions and limitations<\/strong><\/a>, the ghosts and ghouls of Sunway Lagoon\u2019s Nights of Fright (NOF) are <strong><a href=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/how-industries-are-roaring-back-to-spur-tourism\/\">on the prowl<\/a><\/strong> again to scare a soul or two!<\/p>\n<p>To bring us through a behind-the-scenes look of the hauntings and scares of Nights of Fright 8 is Noor Aishah Ahmad, manager of events and entertainment for Sunway Theme Parks.<\/p>\n<p>From being a visitor at the first Nights of Frights\u00a0 to becoming a part of the team, Aishah\u2019s vast experience both as a talent and performer has help her \u00a0rise through the ranks. She now \u00a0oversees \u00a0the entire ghostly experience and ensuring each guest has a screaming good time!<\/p>\n<p><strong>6.30am<br \/>\n<\/strong>I wake up fairly early as it takes me awhile to get to <strong><a href=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/the-efforts-that-made-sunway-city-kuala-lumpur-the-self-sustaining-city-it-is-today\/\">Sunway City Kuala Lumpur<\/a><\/strong> (SCKL) from where I live, especially during rush hour.<\/p>\n<p><strong>8.00am<br \/>\n<\/strong>My day in the office begins bright and early, and I make sure to have a hearty breakfast to prepare for a hectic ahead!<\/p>\n<p><strong>9.00am<\/strong><\/p>\n<div id=\"attachment_28874\" style=\"width: 1210px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-28874\" class=\"size-full wp-image-28874\" src=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/2.jpg\" alt=\"Mid shot of Aishah regrouping with the team in the Sunway Lagoon meeting room.\" width=\"1200\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/2-200x133.jpg 200w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/2-314x209.jpg 314w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/2-400x267.jpg 400w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/2-600x400.jpg 600w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/2-768x512.jpg 768w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/2-800x533.jpg 800w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/2-942x628.jpg 942w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/2.jpg 1200w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" \/><p id=\"caption-attachment-28874\" class=\"wp-caption-text\">Regrouping with the team first thing in the morning is important for us to improve<\/p><\/div>\n<p>Morning meetings with operation leaders of the theme park covers deadlines, any concerns that have risen within the theme park \u2013 and how we can improve. All these happen before our park\u2019s opening hour!<\/p>\n<p>Music? Check. Costumes? Check. Mascots \u2013 are Captain and Lady Quack here? Yes? We are ready to go!<\/p>\n<p><strong>1.50pm<br \/>\n<\/strong>We are about four hours to showtime and need to do our check and follow-up. My team and I get together to discuss upcoming events and functions, check on our deadlines and progress and to ensure everything is in order. This is when we run through our shows for the night, music selection, choreography and staging!<\/p>\n<div id=\"attachment_28875\" style=\"width: 1210px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-28875\" class=\"size-full wp-image-28875\" src=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/3.jpg\" alt=\"The Sunway Lagoon dancers posing in black, undead attires for the upcoming Nights of Fright.\" width=\"1200\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/3-200x133.jpg 200w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/3-314x209.jpg 314w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/3-400x267.jpg 400w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/3-600x400.jpg 600w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/3-768x512.jpg 768w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/3-800x533.jpg 800w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/3-942x628.jpg 942w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/3.jpg 1200w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" \/><p id=\"caption-attachment-28875\" class=\"wp-caption-text\">Practice makes perfect! We go through the choreography once before we open for the night<\/p><\/div>\n<p>Any last-minute additions or dance rehearsals are also finalised by now so that we are all in sync for the night. As I also manage Screamfest\u00a0 at <a href=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/rediscovering-a-lost-world\/\"><strong>The Lost World of Tambun<\/strong><\/a> in Sunway City Ipoh, I have to speak with the team to ensure everything is in order. It is our first time organising Screamfest and we have been experiencing a great reception so far!<\/p>\n<p><strong>5.00pm<\/strong><\/p>\n<div id=\"attachment_28876\" style=\"width: 1210px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-28876\" class=\"size-full wp-image-28876\" src=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/4.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1200\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/4-200x133.jpg 200w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/4-314x209.jpg 314w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/4-400x267.jpg 400w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/4-600x400.jpg 600w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/4-768x512.jpg 768w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/4-800x533.jpg 800w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/4-942x628.jpg 942w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/4.jpg 1200w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" \/><p id=\"caption-attachment-28876\" class=\"wp-caption-text\">One last meeting, makeup check and we are ready to go!<\/p><\/div>\n<p>It is now time to transform ourselves into characters assigned \u2013 this starts with yet another meeting with our full-time team and part timers who have graciously joined us as one of the undead for Nights of Fright. Once the briefing is complete, off we go to costumes, hair and make-up.<\/p>\n<p>Whether a zombie, werewolf or some other ghastly creature \u2013 we have to be ready by 6pm sharp!<\/p>\n<p><strong>6.15pm<br \/>\n<\/strong>The undead is now amidst the living! In our full costumes, we head to Sunway Pyramid for a flash mob to draw in the crowd for a sneak preview of our spooky spectacular later that night!<\/p>\n<p>If you see us, don\u2019t run \u2013 we just want to have a little bit of fun!<\/p>\n<p><strong>7.00pm<br \/>\n<\/strong>After the flash mob, it\u2019s back to the theme park to do final checks on lights, setup, ambience and safety \u2013 which is our utmost priority. I make sure that each teammate has proper rest and a hearty dinner as they will most likely be on their feet the rest of the night.<\/p>\n<div id=\"attachment_28877\" style=\"width: 1210px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-28877\" class=\"size-full wp-image-28877\" src=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/5.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1200\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/5-200x133.jpg 200w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/5-314x209.jpg 314w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/5-400x267.jpg 400w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/5-600x400.jpg 600w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/5-768x512.jpg 768w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/5-800x533.jpg 800w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/5-942x628.jpg 942w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/5.jpg 1200w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" \/><p id=\"caption-attachment-28877\" class=\"wp-caption-text\">The countdown to the gates of horror begin at 730pm, are you ready?<\/p><\/div>\n<p><strong>7.25pm<br \/>\n<\/strong>The countdown to the night of devilishly good fun begins! Tick tock tick tock\u2026<\/p>\n<p><strong>7.30pm<br \/>\n<\/strong>The gates are now open! Come one, come all \u2013 explore each and every one of our eight haunted houses; step into our haunted theatre or test your bravery at our two scare zones! If all things spooky are not your cup of tea, you can still have fun at any of our 11 thrill rides that are open within the theme park or enjoy any of our six shows on our Nights of Fright Main Stage or Pirate Stage. For the next few hours, it is my duty to oversee all of the operations with my team, and to make sure everyone is having a safe and terrifyingly good time.<\/p>\n<div id=\"attachment_28878\" style=\"width: 1210px\" class=\"wp-caption aligncenter\"><img decoding=\"async\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-28878\" class=\"size-full wp-image-28878\" src=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/6.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1200\" height=\"665\" srcset=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/6-200x111.png 200w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/6-377x209.png 377w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/6-400x222.png 400w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/6-600x333.png 600w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/6-768x426.png 768w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/6-800x443.png 800w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/6-1133x628.png 1133w, https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/wp-content\/uploads\/2022\/11\/6.png 1200w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" \/><p id=\"caption-attachment-28878\" class=\"wp-caption-text\">With six performances planned for each night, we make sure that all of our actors and teammates are well rested and fed prior hitting the stage!<\/p><\/div>\n<p><strong>11.15pm<br \/>\n<\/strong>What a night! We wrap up with a party where NOF characters tear up the dance floor with our guests, ending the night on a high!<\/p>\n<p>Werewolves, zombies and other creatures are here to send off our guests \u2013 before the night ends, my team and I scour the park to ensure all guests leave the park safe and sound, and that the cleanliness of the theme park is maintained.<\/p>\n<p><strong>12.30am<br \/>\n<\/strong>Once completed, I run through the items of the day to be reviewed so we can address this when the work day starts all over again. Time to retire for the night. 😉<\/p>\n","protected":false},"excerpt":{"rendered":"<div class='heateorSssClear'><\/div><div class='heateor_sss_sharing_container heateor_sss_horizontal_sharing' in the Spotlight"},"content":{"rendered":"<p><em>In this Q&A segment, <\/em>Berita Sunway<em> gets to know the leaders across Sunway Group<\/em><\/p>\n<p><strong>Danial Abdul Rahman, Director of Sunway Education Group CEO\u2019s office<\/strong><\/p>\n<p><strong>Eleanor Choong, Chief operating officer of Sunway XFarms<\/strong><\/p>\n<p><strong>Letchumy Adekan, Director of Information Technology Shared Services\u00a0Centre at Sunway Group<\/strong><\/p>\n<h5><strong>1. What do you enjoy most about your job?<\/strong><\/h5>\n<p><strong>Danial:<\/strong> Being able to work with a diverse team of talented individuals, meeting potential collaborators and partners, as well as supporting student development and growth.<\/p>\n<p><strong>Eleanor:<\/strong> I\u2019ve spent years working with intangible digital products so I love the idea that as farmers, we get to use our skills and time to literally <a href=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/sowing-seeds-of-kindness-this-lunar-new-year\/\"><strong>sow seeds<\/strong><\/a> and see them come to life. It\u2019s fulfilling to know that we are nourishing our customers with safe and fresh food, making an impact in the health and wellbeing of our communities. Every minute spent on work is a step closer towards improving food security in Malaysia.<\/p>\n<p><strong>Letchumy:<\/strong> I enjoy the versatility of being able to handle a variety of digitalisation initiatives and working with various businesses across Sunway. Besides being a part of the Group\u2019s new digitalisation adoption, driving various IT projects from ideation to launch brings me great satisfaction, especially seeing businesses across Sunway benefit from the <a href=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/sunway-x-huawei-upping-digital-innovation\/\"><strong>innovations<\/strong><\/a>, and how it transforms users\u2019 experience. Of course, it is a joy to work alongside collaborative and supportive leaders across the Group.<\/p>\n<h5><strong>2. What is the most challenging part of your job?<\/strong><\/h5>\n<p><strong>Danial:<\/strong> Being part of the Sunway Education Group (SEG) COVID-19 Management Committee over the last two years \u2013 ensuring that government SOPs are properly interpreted, communicated, and implemented across the campus. Many hours were spent discussing the constantly changing rules from the original lockdown, to the National Recovery Plan and <a href=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/injecting-hope-sunway-steps-up-to-keep-the-nation-safe\/\"><strong>encouraging vaccinations<\/strong><\/a>, as well as preparing the campus for the current endemic phase. All in all, my role in preparing the COVID-19 Advisories (53 and counting!) to ensure a safe university and college experience for all has been truly rewarding.<\/p>\n<p><strong>Eleanor:<\/strong> Leafy vegetables are fragile and need tender loving care. During the pandemic, <a href=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/the-new-garden-of-eden\/\"><strong>our farms<\/strong><\/a> continued operating and our teams travelled to work daily. We are always on alert to monitor the health of our farms, and to ensure that our vegetables are healthy and happy 24\/7.\u00a0Our next biggest milestone would be to launch Sunway XFarms @ Sunway Tower, the largest indoor vertical farm in KLCC.<\/p>\n<p><strong>Letchumy:<\/strong> Keeping people on the same page when it comes to decisions, alignment, goals, direction, culture, and team spirit. It requires strong strategies to ensure the whole team is on board. I view this as a crucial part of my leadership, so I make the effort to be on the ground and take the necessary steps to ensure it.<\/p>\n<h5><strong>3. What is your best management decision? And your worst?<\/strong><\/h5>\n<p><strong>Danial:<\/strong> The best was the collective decision to allow students with needs to access the campus during the various MCOs to ensure learning continuity. This required essential staff to be present on campus to provide essential services. It was truly inspiring to see it all come together in the end.<\/p>\n<p>The worst was in a previous job, I had hired and trusted someone who unfortunately abused their position for self-enrichment. Police reports were lodged, and it was an unpleasant experience all round. It taught me to ensure better due diligence when hiring, and that trust is a premium.<\/p>\n<p><strong>Eleanor:<\/strong> Recruiting an amazing team was by far my best management decision to date. They are humble, hardworking, fun and 100% committed to their work, which brings out the best in one another.<\/p>\n<p>My worst would probably include some of the decisions I made during our first year of launching <a href=\"https:\/\/www.amirulashraf.my\/stories\/farm-in-a-city\/\"><strong>Sunway XFarms<\/strong><\/a>. We were constantly exploring various products, business models and service options without a key vision and identity. This stretched the team beyond their abilities without giving them sufficient space and time to grow and thrive.<\/p>\n<p><strong>Letchumy:<\/strong> I decided that the best thing that I could do for myself, and the company, was to delegate. I strive to empower my subordinates so that I can focus on areas that matter most in my current role.<\/p>\n<p>The worst decision was when I decided to swap out a person whom I felt was not working very well on a project. I later discovered that the same person performed tremendously in another project. Had I invested a little time to guide and coach the person at the right time, it would have made all the difference.<\/p>\n<h5><strong>4. What is the best management advice you\u2019ve received?<\/strong><\/h5>\n<p><strong>Danial:<\/strong> \u201cKnowledge is a trust. Don\u2019t just keep it to yourself, find ways to impart it to the next generation\u201d. This is the reason why I\u2019ve been in the education space for the longest time in my career.<\/p>\n<p><strong>Eleanor: <\/strong>\u201cLet us run with endurance the race that is set before us\u201d.\u00a0 That we see our purpose in life as a marathon and run each step with strength, endurance, faith and hope. Rather than focus on the ups and downs in the short term, I try to focus on the long-term vision of why we do what we do, and how we can constantly learn from our failures and advance ahead with boldness.<\/p>\n<p><strong>Letchumy: <\/strong>\u201cSuccess is made by many and not all by yourself.\u00a0 Get to know your people well and use the right resources to get things done\u201d.\u00a0 I learnt that I cannot do it all by myself and need to invest my time in getting to know the people within and outside the organisation who can be a part of my success.<\/p>\n<h5><strong>5. How do you unwind after work or on the weekends?<\/strong><\/h5>\n<p><strong>Danial:<\/strong> Spending time with family, playing badminton or going for a run.\u00a0 I am also passionate about my two cats, Ram and Mo. My wife and I co-manage their Instagram account. Do follow them @tuanramses, as it would make them happy!<\/p>\n<p><strong>Eleanor:<\/strong> As a mom of two young kids and two furkids, I don\u2019t exactly get to go home, turn on \u2018airplane\u2019 mode and declare the day over. My very colourful kids keep me busy in the evenings and weekends, but they are my source of inspiration and in a way, seeing them safe and happy is what I find comfort in.<\/p>\n<p><strong>Letchumy: <\/strong>I enjoy cooking more elaborate meals for my family over the weekend and planning family trips. For my self-care, I find time to exercise and spend time in solitude especially if I need to get a different perspective on things.\u00a0 It works well for me for a fresh start to the day or week.<\/p>\n","protected":false},"excerpt":{"rendered":"<div class='heateorSssClear'><\/div><div class='heateor_sss_sharing_container heateor_sss_horizontal_sharing'
